## Recommendations

1. Wrap all user-facing text in `t()` function calls
2. Add translation keys to `src/i18n/locales/en.ts` and `src/i18n/locales/fr.ts`
3. Use descriptive translation keys (e.g., `common.button.submit`)
4. Test language switching to ensure all text is translated
